  <span m='1919600'>cusps,</span> <span m='1920710'>we</span> <span m='1920800'>encounter</span>
  <span m='1921550'>bifurcations</span> <span m='1922660'>in</span> <span m='1922810'>the</span>
  <span m='1922900'>solution.</span> <span m='1923480'>So</span> <span m='1923560'>we</span>
